<review>We got lucky and didn't encounter huge crowds, tho I can image this hike gets a lot of traffic.  It's shaded, lush, gentle at the start with a nice climb down to the waterfall and back- nothing too hard so good for all ages - although some parts of it are narrow with a steep drop. Hubby went swimming in the pool under the waterfall- too cold for me!<//review>< pictures>

< Review>
I really enjoy this magnificent trail. It was a short moderate hike. On your way to the waterfall it's easy however on your way back you'll encounter a few inclines. Other than that a beautiful trail. The best views of the Angeles Forest mountains</Review>

< review>
When I went, it was a bit busy. I arrived around 7:05am and the gates were closed to the trail entrance parking area, or picnic¬† area, it just closed for the cars,¬† so¬† I had to park at the parking spots by the road and walked down to the tail entrance, which is around the picnic area,

If you see the sign ‚ÄúSwitzer Picnic Area‚Äù, there is a pathway that takes you down to the trail entrance.
Also you will walk next to the creek no against the¬† creek, however you will cross the river and you will face (2)trails¬† I will recommend the top trail, if you're a beginning hiker, is so much easier eventhough have some inclination but you wil be able to do it. , but if you desire to take down trail¬† becareful you will have to climb a rocks ddownhill.
If You took top trail After 2.5 miles you will have to take downhill you will see a sign that said falls, follow the sign and you will face the waterfall so you will walk against the the creek.
Note : Important¬† you can go back the way you get in there or you can go back by hiking by the top of the of the waterfall but is so hard you will have to climb a rocks uphill, there is water on the rocks I will no recommend.

The trail is primarily used for hiking and is accessible year-round. Dogs are also able to use this trail but must be kept on leash.

The way down isn‚Äôt too bad.¬† I did 5 miles , Returning was more strenuous than going to the falls.. The waterfall was beautiful and the trail was mostly shady and cool breeze made our hike more enjoyable.

smooth walk it‚Äôs just only the way back that there‚Äôs inclinationat the end.¬† River crossing but there big enough rocks to make it through just fine! Enjoy!¬† PLEASE KEEP IT¬† CLEAN THIS TRAIL , PLEASE DON'T SIGH YOUR STUPI NAME ON IT ROCKS , NO GRAFFITI PLEASE< /review>

< text>
It has something for everyone !
First part of the trail is easy but as you start going up, you go up for a while and then down on a busy and narrow trail till you get to waterfalls.

Many people with üêï  and seen many without a leash. Is a trail for all ages.
Beautiful place.<//text>

< review>
The trail to Switzer fall for most part is easy. Lots of water crossing and rock hopping back and forth. At about 1 mile in before you begin the the incline, you can follow the stream to get a view of the top of Switzer fall. Turn around and go back up the trail. Once you get to the top and start your decent down the trail to the fall, more stream crossing and rock hopping. you will see your first fall. This is where most people stop have snack take pictures.  But it's not Switzer fall. If you are adventures you can clime the right side of the fall and keep going up stream for about 5 minutes hike and you will be at Switzer fall.<//review>

<review>This is a wonderful hotel with a beautiful view of a lake.  The staff is very friendly and the cleaning of the rooms are daily.  The rooms are spacious and business grade.  You have free wi-fi, ice, central heating/air, clean linen, adjustable beds (sleep number), coffee maker, alarm clock radio, hair dryer, shampoo, conditioner, lotion and soap.  The view of the lake was grand with a fountain, geese on the water, a Koi fish pond with it's own fountain and a nice pathway.  The hotel also has a swimming pool with a safety fence a small amphitheater area with soft music coming through speakers when not in use. There are ice rooms located around the property with soda machines.

The convention rooms are elegant and host many events. There is a Grill that serves and offers room service, a Bar but my favorite is the dining room.  The breakfasts were fresh cooked daily whether it was served or buffet and refilled often.  The morning servers along with the chef and cooks were very friendly and personable. They were my favorite part of the experience not excluding Sylvia at the front desk.

The rooms are very clean along with their bathrooms. Because of the fear of bed bugs in some of the local motels and extended stay hotels this was a pleasant experience. alleviating those concerns. All concerns are addressed immediately (not that there should be any but things can happen).

Do be aware that during the wet season it tended to flood in front of the entrance to the hotel's property. (This might have been addressed by now)

This hotel is a definite Yes and a Must Try.< /review>< Rate>

< review>
An unexpected but pleasant little restaurant located on the side of a quiet stripmall, Vinter's Tavern creates a rustic and cozy environment, perfect for groups or couples looking to enjoy a night out. As soon as we entered, we were greeted by our friendly host and serenaded with live music coming.

We were seated in the smaller alcove sectioned room with only 3 other tables which was nice. I don't think that room is normally open because there was air conditioning parts laying around but it works out because the main area was quite loud.

We ordered a flight of Wine and for starters, we ordered the bone marrow and the mussels, for mains we tried the vegetable melange and Vinter's Burger and finished the meal off with the. Creme brule.  The food was good but it doesn't match up to other fine dining restaurants. The Creme brule was the weakest part of the meal.< /review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
I have been cycling for several years now.  And, I am definitely NOT a cycling guru.  So, I shopped around and had a ton of work done at different places over a span of about three years.  Then, after many hundreds of dollars and several different places later, I found Mark's Bicycle Shop.  It was  recommended to me by a friend.  Although prior recommendations about other bicycle shops never panned out, I thought, what the heck.

Let me just tell you, Mark and his staff are by far the best and most attentive staff of any bicycle shop that I have ever frequented.  It's got that "mom and pop" feel, but is very professional, and competitive in price and selection.  I have done everything through this shop concerning my bicycle, and riding, from purchasing gear all the way to having a yearly full service done to my bicycles.  I am never unsatisfied, even one bit.

The best part is, Mark takes pride in everything that he does.  This definitely rubs off on his staff.  All of the personnel that he hires has extensive knowledge about cycling, and treats customers with the utmost care and respect.  If you were like me, taking your bicycle to a larger chain store, and have been dissatisfied, my recommendation would be to try out Mark's shop.  Far and above one of the best businesses in all of Rancho Cucamonga.

They have a loyal customer in me, that's for sure.<//Review>

<Review>We have been going here ever since they opened, 30+ years ago. This is the go to spot on Ojai. Every time my family comes home to visit we always end up here. We have celebrated many special occasions here and love to come anytime. The breakfast is great too!

That's some mighty fresh fish that makes up the bulk of their menu.
